Power BI Developer - iDatalytics Pvt. Ltd.

About iDatalytics Pvt. Ltd.: iDatalytics Pvt. Ltd. is a global digital consulting and delivery organization with a core focus on AI, ML, BI, and Analytics. We help organizations work smarter and grow faster by enabling their digital transformation initiatives. Our mission is to serve as a catalyst for digital transformation for our clients.

Role Overview: We are seeking a hands-on, experienced Power BI Developer who can understand business requirements in a BI context and design data models to derive significant insights. This role is crucial for transforming raw data into actionable intelligence.

Details: * Designation: Power BI Developer * Qualification: B. Tech * Experience: 4-6 Years * Skills: Power BI, Oracle, SQL, Tableau, Qlik, ETL * Remuneration: Salary is negotiable and will be best in the industry. * Location: Infopark, Phase 2, Jyothirmaya Building, 1st Floor, Kakkanad.

Role Description: * Understand business requirements in the BI context and design data models to convert raw data into meaningful insights. * Create dashboards and interactive visual reports using Power BI. * Identify Key Performance Indicators (KPIs) with clear objectives and monitor them consistently. * Analyze data and present it through reports that aid in decision-making. * Convert business requirements into technical specifications and define task timelines. * Design, develop, and deploy Power BI scripts and perform efficient detailed analysis. * Perform DAX queries and functions within Power BI. * Create charts and document data with explanations of algorithms, parameters, models, and relations. * Perform SQL querying for optimal results. * Utilize filters and graphs for enhanced data understanding. * Define and design new systems by analyzing current ETL processes. * Implement technical changes to existing BI systems to improve functionality.

Non-technical (soft) skills: * Ability to interact effectively with both business and technical teams. * Comprehensive knowledge of data design, data modeling, data management, and data visualization. * Strong communication and client management skills. * Stay updated with advancements and best practices in design and development. * Document processes, models, designs, and solutions, and effectively explain them to the team. * Apply learned lessons to future solution considerations. * Possess an analytical mindset with a problem-solving approach. * Ability to work in an agile environment with a focus on continuous improvement. * Self-motivated and eager to learn.

Skills and Experience: * Excellent knowledge of Power BI & related tools (PBI desktop & service, tabular editor, DAX studio, etc.). * Very good data transformation skills using ETL tools (Azure Data Factory, SQL Server SSIS, PowerQuery, Informatica, Databricks experience would be an asset). * Solid working knowledge of SQL and relational databases (ideally MS SQL or Azure Synapse Analytics). * Hands-on working experience in a CI/CD-supported Azure data warehouse environment. * Familiarity with iterative development & Agile concepts and adaptability to changing requirements. * Strong self-motivation and problem-solving skills with a sense of ownership and delivery focus. * Strong written and verbal communication skills. * Ability to translate information simply and clearly to business stakeholders. * Proven experience as a Power BI Developer or in a similar role. * Strong understanding of Power BI, including Power Query, DAX, and visualization best practices. * Hands-on experience with database management systems like SQL Server or other relational databases.

Technical Skills: * Proficiency in Microsoft Power BI Desktop and Power BI Service. * Knowledge of ETL processes and tools. * Familiarity with other BI tools (e.g., Tableau, Qlik) is a plus. * Experience with programming languages like Python or R is advantageous.

Contact: If interested, please share your updated resume to hr@idatalytics.com

Thanks and regards, HR Team
